import os
import re

pages_dir = 'src/pages'

for filename in os.listdir(pages_dir):
    if not filename.endswith('.tsx'):
        continue
    path = os.path.join(pages_dir, filename)
    with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    if 'PageMeta' not in content:
        continue
    
    # Replace the return block: wrap PageMeta and MainLayout in <>
    # Find pattern: return (
    #   <PageMeta ... />
    #   <MainLayout>
    # and replace with: return (
    #   <>
    #     <PageMeta ... />
    #     <MainLayout>
    
    # Then find the matching </MainLayout>\n  ); and replace with </MainLayout>\n  </>\n  );
    
    # First, add opening fragment
    content = re.sub(
        r'(return \(\n)(\s*)(<PageMeta\s+title=\{t\(\'[^\']+\'\)\}\s+description=\{t\(\'[^\']+\'\)\}\s*/>\n)(\s*)(<MainLayout>)',
        r'\1\2<>\n\2  \3\4\5',
        content
    )
    
    # Then add closing fragment before the final closing parenthesis
    # Pattern: </MainLayout>\n  );
    content = re.sub(
        r'(\s*)(</MainLayout>)(\n\s*)\);',
        r'\1\2\3  </>\3);',
        content
    )
    
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(content)
    print(f'Fixed {filename}')

COMMAND:
cd /workspace/app-cku4hf2twpvl && cat > /tmp/fix_pagemeta3.py << 'PYEOF'
import os
import re

pages_dir = 'src/pages'

for filename in os.listdir(pages_dir):
    if not filename.endswith('.tsx'):
        continue
    path = os.path.join(pages_dir, filename)
    with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # Fix escaped quotes from bad regex
    content = content.replace(r"t(\'", "t(")
    content = content.replace(r"'\')}", "')}")
    
    # Fix indentation: ensure <> and </> have same indentation as return
    # We'll normalize by replacing the bad indentation block
    # Pattern: return (\n          <>\n            <PageMeta ... />\n            <MainLayout>
    # Should be: return (\n    <>\n      <PageMeta ... />\n      <MainLayout>
    
    content = re.sub(
        r'(return \(\n)\s+<>(\n\s+)(<PageMeta\s+title=\{t\([^\)]+\)\}\s+description=\{t\([^\)]+\)\}\s+/>)(\n\s+)(<MainLayout>)',
        lambda m: f"{m.group(1)}    <>\n      {m.group(3)}\n      {m.group(5)}",
        content
    )
    
    # Fix closing fragment indentation
    # Pattern: </MainLayout>\n  </>\n  );  -> good
    # Pattern: </MainLayout>\n    </>\n    );  -> ensure consistent
    content = re.sub(
        r'(\s+)(</MainLayout>)(\n\s+)(</>)(\n\s+)\);',
        lambda m: f"\n    {m.group(2)}\n  {m.group(4)}\n  );",
        content
    )
    
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(content)
    print(f'Cleaned {filename}')

COMMAND:
cd /workspace/app-cku4hf2twpvl && cat > /tmp/clean_pagemeta.py << 'PYEOF'
import os
import re

pages_dir = 'src/pages'

for filename in os.listdir(pages_dir):
    if not filename.endswith('.tsx'):
        continue
    path = os.path.join(pages_dir, filename)
    with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # Remove PageMeta import line
    content = re.sub(r"^import PageMeta from '@/components/common/PageMeta';\n", '', content, flags=re.MULTILINE)
    
    # Remove PageMeta component block (multiline, flexible spacing)
    content = re.sub(
        r"\s*<PageMeta\s+title=\{t\([^\}]+\)\}\s+description=\{t\([^\}]+\)\}\s*/>\n",
        '\n',
        content
    )
    
    # Remove fragment wrappers added by previous script
    content = content.replace('return (\n    <>\n', 'return (\n')
    content = content.replace('return (\n          <>\n', 'return (\n')
    content = re.sub(r"\n\s*</>\n\s*\);", '\n  );', content)
    
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(content)
    print(f'Cleaned {filename}')

COMMAND:
cd /workspace/app-cku4hf2twpvl && cat > /tmp/add_pagemeta_v2.py << 'PYEOF'
import os
import re

pages_dir = 'src/pages'

page_configs = {
    'CalculatorPage.tsx': 'support_calculator',
    'CareersPage.tsx': 'careers',
    'CertificatesPage.tsx': 'about_certificates',
    'ContactPage.tsx': 'contact',
    'DownloadsPage.tsx': 'support_downloads',
    'FaqPage.tsx': 'support_faq',
    'HistoryPage.tsx': 'about_history',
    'HomePage.tsx': 'home',
    'NewsDetailPage.tsx': 'news_detail',
    'NewsPage.tsx': 'news',
    'NotFound.tsx': 'not_found',
    'ProductDetailPage.tsx': 'product_detail',
    'ProductionPage.tsx': 'about_production',
    'ProductsPage.tsx': 'products',
    'ProfilePage.tsx': 'about_profile',
    'QualityPage.tsx': 'quality',
    'SoftwarePage.tsx': 'support_software',
}

for filename, seo_key in page_configs.items():
    path = os.path.join(pages_dir, filename)
    with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # Skip if already has PageMeta
    if 'PageMeta' in content:
        print(f'Skip {filename}')
        continue
    
    # Add import line after useTranslation import
    import_line = "import PageMeta from '@/components/common/PageMeta';\n"
    if "import { useTranslation } from '@/data/i18n';" in content:
        content = content.replace(
            "import { useTranslation } from '@/data/i18n';\n",
            "import { useTranslation } from '@/data/i18n';\n" + import_line
        )
    else:
        content = content.replace(
            "import MainLayout from '@/components/layouts/MainLayout';\n",
            "import MainLayout from '@/components/layouts/MainLayout';\n" + import_line
        )
    
    # Add PageMeta as first child of MainLayout
    pagemeta = f"""      <PageMeta
        title={{t('seo_{seo_key}_title')}}
        description={{t('seo_{seo_key}_desc')}}
      />\n"""
    content = re.sub(r'(<MainLayout>\n)', r'\1' + pagemeta, content, count=1)
    
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(content)
    print(f'Updated {filename}')
PYEOF
python3 /tmp/add_pagemeta_v2.py

Created File with Text:
```
# 家和自动化官网部署说明

## 一、部署前准备

1. 确保已有自己的域名（如 `www.jiahe-auto.com`）并已解析到服务器。
2. 准备一台可以访问互联网的 Linux 服务器（推荐 Ubuntu 22.04 LTS）。
3. 在服务器上安装 Nginx：
   ```bash
   sudo apt update
   sudo apt install nginx
   ```
4. 准备 SSL 证书（推荐使用 Let's Encrypt / Certbot 免费证书）。

## 二、修改配置

在此文件夹中需要替换域名的地方：

1. `nginx.conf`
   - 将 `www.example.com` 和 `example.com` 替换为你的实际域名。
   - 将 `/var/www/jiahe-website/dist` 替换为你的实际部署路径。
   - 如需 HTTPS，取消 HTTPS 服务块的注释，并填入证书路径。

2. `../public/robots.txt`
   - 将 `https://www.example.com/sitemap.xml` 替换为你的实际域名地址。

3. `../public/sitemap.xml`
   - 将 `https://www.example.com` 替换为你的实际域名。
   - 如有新增或删除页面，及时更新 `<url>` 节点。

## 三、构建项目

在项目根目录执行：

```bash
npm run build
```

构建完成后，会在项目根目录下生成 `dist/` 文件夹。

## 四、部署到服务器

### 方式一：手动上传

```bash
# 将本地 dist 上传到服务器（修改为你的服务器 IP 和路径）
scp -r dist root@your-server-ip:/var/www/jiahe-website/
```

### 方式二：CI/CD 自动部署

可以配合 GitHub Actions / GitLab CI 在代码推送后自动构建并部署到服务器。

## 五、配置 Nginx

1. 将 `nginx.conf` 复制到 Nginx 配置目录：
   ```bash
   sudo cp deploy/nginx.conf /etc/nginx/sites-available/jiahe-website
   sudo ln -s /etc/nginx/sites-available/jiahe-website /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/
   sudo nginx -t
   sudo systemctl reload nginx
   ```

2. 如使用 Let's Encrypt 证书，运行：
   ```bash
   sudo apt install certbot python3-certbot-nginx
   sudo certbot --nginx -d www.example.com -d example.com
   ```

## 六、提交搜索引擎收录

### 百度
1. 访问 https://ziyuan.baidu.com 
2. 添加网站（使用域名或站点验证）。
3. 在「网站支持 → sitemap」中提交：`https://www.example.com/sitemap.xml`。
4. 在「快速收录 → 链接提交」中提交首页和重要产品页面。

### Google
1. 访问 https://search.google.com/search-console 
2. 添加属性（域名验证推荐）。
3. 在「Sitemaps」中提交：`https://www.example.com/sitemap.xml`。
4. 等待 Google 爬虫自然抓取。

### Bing
1. 访问 https://www.bing.com/webmasters 
2. 添加站点并验证。
3. 提交 sitemap。

## 七、部署后验证

1. 访问域名首页，确认页面正常显示。
2. 检查源代码 `<title>` 和 `<meta name="description">` 是否正确。
3. 访问 `https://www.example.com/sitemap.xml` 确认 sitemap 可访问。
4. 访问 `https://www.example.com/robots.txt` 确认 robots.txt 可访问。

```

|\n| `data.Pages` | number | 总页数 |\n| `data.Uv` | string | 预估流量范围 |\n| `data.Total` | number | 总条数 |\n| `data.Count` | number | 当前页条数 |\n| `data.Domain` | string | 查询域名 |\n| `data.Current` | number | 当前页码 |\n| `data.List[].RankStr` | string | 排名（如 "1-2" 表示排名区间） |\n| `data.List[].SiteCount` | number | 收录量 |\n| `data.List[].Keyword` | string | 关键词 |\n| `data.List[].Calalog` | string | 目录路径 |\n| `data.List[].Title` | string | 页面标题 |\n| `data.List[].Index` | number | PC 指数 |\n| `data.List[].Url` | string | 标题链接 |\n\n**错误码：**\n\n| code | 说明 |\n|------|------|\n| 200 | 成功 |\n| 400 | 参数错误（如域名为空） |\n| 500 | 系统维护，请稍候再试 |\n| 999 | 其他错误，以实际返回为准 |\n\n## 生成期用法（Agent 直接调用）\n\n```typescript\nconst apiKey = process.env["INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY"]!; // platform_managed 密钥由平台注入\n\ninterface KeywordItem {\n string;\n  Total: number;\n  Count: number;\n  Domain: string;\n  Current: number;\n  List: KeywordItem[];\n}\n\n/**\n * 查询指定域名在百度PC端的关键词排名数据。\n * @param domain - 查询的域名，例如 "www.example.com"\n * @param catalog - 可选，目录名称，默认选择全部数据\n * @param page - 可选，分页页码，默认第 1 页\n * @returns 关键词排名数据对象\n */\nasync function queryBaiduPcKeywordRanking(\n  domain: string,\n  catalog?: string,\n  page?: string,\n): Promise<KeywordRankingData> {\n  const params: Record<string, string> = { domain };\n  if (catalog) params.catalog = catalog;\n  if (page) params.page = page;\n\n  const response = await fetch(\n    "https://app-cku4hf2twpvl-api-DLEO4zmpN5ja-gateway.appmiaoda.com/seo/baidu/pc/keyword",\n    {\n      method: "POST",\n      headers: {\n        "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",\n        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,\n      },\n      body: new URLSearchParams(params).toString(),\n    },\n  );\n\n  if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP error: "https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts";\n\nserve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {\n  if (req.method !== "POST") {\n    return new Response("Method Not Allowed", { status: 405 });\n  }\n\n  // --- 解析客户端请求 ---\n  let domain: string;\n  let catalog: string | undefined;\n  let page: string | undefined;\n  try {\n    const body = await req.json();\n    domain = body.domain;\n    if (!domain) Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "Server configuration error" }), {\n      status: 500,\n      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n    });\n  }\n\n  // --- 构建请求参数 ---\n  const params: "https://app-cku4hf2twpvl-api-DLEO4zmpN5ja-gateway.appmiaoda.com/seo/baidu/pc/keyword",\n    {\n      method: "POST",\n      headers: {\n        "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",\n        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,\n      },\n      body: new URLSearchParams(params).toString(),\n    },\n  );\n\n  // 转发配额/余额错误\n  if (upstream.status === 429 || upstream.status === 402) {\n    const errText = await upstream.text();\n    return new Response(errText, {\n      status: upstream.status,\n      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n    });\n  }\n\n  if (!upstream.ok) {\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({ error: `Upstream error: ${upstream.status}` }),\n      { status: 502, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" } },\n    );\n  }\n\n  const data = await upstream.json();\n  return new Response(JSON.stringify(data), {\n    status: 200,\n    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n  });\n});\n```\n\n### 前端调用\n\n**推荐方式（supabase client 可用时）：**\n\n```typescript\n/**\n * 通过 Edge Function 查询百度PC关键词排名。\n * @param domain - 查询的域名\n * @param catalog - 可选，目录名称\n * @param page - 可选，分页页码\n * @returns 关键词排名数据对象\n `${import.meta.env.VITE_SUPABASE_URL}/functions/v1/baidu-seo-keyword-ranking`,\n    {\n      method: "POST",\n      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n      body: JSON.stringify({ 402) {\n    const err = await res.json();\n    throw new Error(`余额不足：${err.message ?? res.statusText}`);\n  }\n  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`请求失败：${res.status}`);\n\n  const json = await res.json();\n  if (json.code !== 200) throw new Error(`API 错误 ${json.code}：${json.msg}`);\n\n  return json.data;\n}\n```\n\n## 注意事项\n\n- **密钥安全**：`INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY` 仅可在 Edge Function 服务端读取，严禁暴露到前端。\n- **错误处理**：务必处理 429（配额超限）和 402（余额不足）两类错误；业务层还需处理 400（域名为空或参数错误）。\n- **计费**：原价 ¥0.90/次，折扣价 ¥0.50/次，建议按需查询，避免不必要的重复调用。\n- **分页**：每页最多返回 100 条数据，若 `data.Pages > 1`，需通过递增 `page` # 家和自动化官网部署说明

## 一、部署前准备

1. 确保已有自己的域名（如 `www.jiahe-auto.com`）并已解析到服务器。
2. 准备一台可以访问互联网的 Linux 服务器（推荐 Ubuntu 22.04 LTS）。
3. 在服务器上安装 Nginx：
   ```bash
   sudo apt update
   sudo apt install nginx
   ```
4. 准备 SSL 证书（推荐使用 Let's Encrypt / Certbot 免费证书）。

## 二、修改配置

在此文件夹中需要替换域名的地方：

1. `nginx.conf`
   - 将 `www.example.com` 和 `example.com` 替换为你的实际域名。
   - 将 `/var/www/jiahe-website/dist` 替换为你的实际部署路径。
   - 如需 HTTPS，取消 HTTPS 服务块的注释，并填入证书路径。

2. `../public/robots.txt`
   - 将 `https://www.example.com/sitemap.xml` 替换为你的实际域名地址。

3. `../public/sitemap.xml`
   - 将 `https://www.example.com` 替换为你的实际域名。
   - 如有新增或删除页面，及时更新 `<url>` 节点。

## 三、构建项目

在项目根目录执行：

```bash
npm run build
```

构建完成后，会在项目根目录下生成 `dist/` 文件夹。

## 四、部署到服务器

# 百度AI搜索接口（SSE 流式）

## API 基本信息

| 字段 | 值 |
|------|----|
| Plugin ID | `be049c59-00cf-420d-b21a-1486dc4c6812` |
| API ID | `api-DYJwo27V8Qya` |
| Endpoint | `POST https://app-cku4hf2twpvl-api-DYJwo27V8Qya-gateway.appmiaoda.com/v2/ai_search/chat/completions` |
| 认证模式 | platform_managed |
| Auth Header | `X-Gateway-Authorization: Bearer <INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY>` |
| Content-Type | `application/json` |
| 响应类型 | SSE 流式（text/event-stream） |
| third_part_domain | `app-cku4hf2twpvl-api-DYJwo27V8Qya-gateway.appmiaoda.com` |

---

## 请求参数表

| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 默认值 | 说明 |
|--------|------|------|--------|------|
| `messages` | array | 是 | — | 搜索输入，role 必须是 user-assistant-user 交替 |
| `messages[].role` | string | 是 | — | 角色设定，可选值：`user`、`assistant` |
| `messages[].content` | string | 是 | — | 对话内容，不能为空 |
| `instruction` | string | 否 | `""` | 人设指令，用于设定输出风格 |
| `enable_deep_search` | boolean | 否 | `false` | 是否开启深搜索（最多 10 次智能搜索，每种类型最多返回 100 个结果） |
| `resource_type_filter` | array | 否 | — | 搜索资源类型过滤 |
| `resource_type_filter[].type` | string | 是 | — | 搜索资源类型：`video`、`image`、`web` |
| `resource_type_filter[].top_k` | integer | 是 | — | 指定模态最大返回个数 |
| `search_recency_filter` | string | 否 | — | 按网页发布时间筛选：`week`、`month`、`semiyear`、`year` |
| `enable_reasoning` | boolean | 否 | `true` | 是否开启深度思考（支持 DeepSeek-R1、文心X1） |
| `max_completion_tokens` | integer | 否 | `2048` | 最大输出 token 数 |
| `response_format` | string | 否 | `auto` | 输出内容样式：`auto`、`text`、`rich_text` |
| `enable_followup_queries` | boolean | 否 | `false` | 是否开启追问建议 |

---

## 响应字段表

### 成功响应（每条 SSE 事件的 data JSON）

| 字段路径 | 类型 | 说明 |
|----------|------|------|
| `is_safe` | boolean | 内容安全标识 |
| `choices` | array | 生成结果数组 |
| `choices[].finish_reason` | string | 结束原因，如 `stop` |
| `choices[].index` | integer | 结果索引 |
| `choices[].delta.content` | string | 本次增量输出内容 |
| `choices[].delta.reasoning_content` | string? | 推理过程增量内容（开启 reasoning 时） |
| `choices[].delta.role` | string | 角色，固定为 `assistant` |
| `usage` | object? | Token 用量统计（最后一条事件携带） |
| `usage.prompt_tokens` | integer | 输入 token 数 |
| `usage.completion_tokens` | integer | 输出 token 数 |
| `usage.total_tokens` | integer | 总 token 数 |
| `references` | array? | 引用来源列表（部分事件携带） |
| `references[].id` | integer | 引用编号 |
| `references[].title` | string | 网页标题 |
| `references[].url` | string | 网页地址 |
| `references[].web_anchor` | string | 网站锚文本 |
| `references[].content` | string | 网站内容摘要 |
| `references[].date` | string | 网页发布日期 |
| `references[].type` | string | 资源类型：`web`、`image`、`video` |
| `followup_queries` | array? | 推荐追问问题列表（开启 enable_followup_queries 时） |

---

## 生成期代码

以下代码可在 Deno 脚本或生成期 Agent 中直接运行，逐行读取 SSE 并累积输出。

```typescript
const apiKey = process.env["INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY"]!; // platform_managed 密钥由平台注入

interface Message {
  role: "user" | "assistant";
  content: string;
}

interface ResourceTypeFilter {
  type: "video" | "image" | "web";
  top_k: number;
}

interface AiSearchRequest {
  messages: Message[];
  instruction?: string;
  enable_deep_search?: boolean;
  resource_type_filter?: ResourceTypeFilter[];
  search_recency_filter?: "week" | "month" | "semiyear" | "year";
  enable_reasoning?: boolean;
  max_completion_tokens?: number;
  response_format?: "auto" | "text" | "rich_text";
  enable_followup_queries?: boolean;
}

/**
 * 调用百度AI搜索接口，流式读取并累积返回全部内容。
 * @param params - 搜索请求参数，messages 必须以 user 角色开头
 * @returns 累积的完整回答文本及最终引用列表
 */
async function callBaiduAiSearch(
  params: AiSearchRequest
): Promise<{ content: string; references: unknown[] }> {
  const response = await fetch(
    "https://app-cku4hf2twpvl-api-DYJwo27V8Qya-gateway.appmiaoda.com/v2/ai_search/chat/completions",
    {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: JSON.stringify(params),
    }
  );

  if (!response.ok) {
    throw new Error(`HTTP error: ${response.status}`);
  }

  const reader = response.body!.getReader();

const apiKey = process.env["INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY"];

async function queryBaiduPcKeywordRanking(domain) {
  const response = await fetch(
    "https://app-cku4hf2twpvl-api-DLEO4zmpN5ja-gateway.appmiaoda.com/seo/baidu/pc/keyword",
    {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: new URLSearchParams({ domain }).toString(),
    }
  );

  if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP error: ${response.status}`);
  const json = await response.json();
  return json;
}

queryBaiduPcKeywordRanking("www.jiahe-auto.com")
  .then(res => console.log("Result for jiahe-auto.com:", JSON.stringify(res)))

import os, re
from html.parser import HTMLParser

base = 'http://www.zuquchina.com'
products = [
    ('74', 'HGH-CA/HGH-HA 系列'),
    ('75', 'HGW-CA/HGW-HA 系列'),
    ('76', 'HGW-CB/HGW-HB 系列'),
    ('77', 'HGW-CC/HGW-HC 系列'),
    ('78', 'HGR-T 下锁式导轨'),
    ('79', 'EGH-SA/EGH-CA 系列'),
    ('80', 'EGW-SA/EGW-CA 系列'),
    ('81', 'EGW-SB/EGW-CB 系列'),
    ('82', 'RGH-CA/RGH-HA 系列'),
    ('83', 'RGL-CA/RGL-HA 系列'),
    ('84', 'RGW-CC/RGW-HC 系列'),
    ('85', 'RGR-T 下锁式滑轨'),
]

class ImgExtractor(HTMLParser):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.imgs = []
        self.current_attrs = {}
    def handle_starttag(self, tag, attrs):
        if tag == 'img':
            d = dict(attrs)
            src = d.get('src', '')
            if src.startswith('/upload/'):
                self.imgs.append(src)

results = {}
for pid, name in products:
    path = f'/tmp/zq_details/{pid}.html'
    with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        html = f.read()
    ext = ImgExtractor()
    ext.feed(html)
    imgs = ext.imgs
    # 过滤掉 logo、备案图标
    imgs = [img for img in imgs if '085250_2_157.png' not in img and '21583110644.png' not in img]
    # 找 product-content 区域的图片
    m = re.search(r'<div class="product-content">(.*?)</div>\s*</div>\s*<div class="row pageturning"', html, re.S)
    content_imgs = []
    if m:
        content_html = m.group(1)
        ext2 = ImgExtractor()
        ext2.feed(content_html)
        content_imgs = [img for img in ext2.imgs if '085250_2_157.png' not in img and '21583110644.png' not in img]
    results[pid] = {'name': name, 'all': imgs, 'content': content_imgs}
    print(f"{pid} {name}")
    print("  all:", imgs)
    print("  content:", content_imgs)
    print()
PYEOF

lines.append("    sub_products: [")
for i, (pid, name) in enumerate(products, 1):
    imgs = content_imgs[pid]
    image_url = base + imgs[0]
    param_images = [base + img for img in imgs[1:]]
    param_str = ', '.join(["'" + url + "'" for url in param_images])
    if param_images:
        line = "      {{ name: '{}', image_url: '{}', sort_order: {}, param_images: [{}] }},".format(name, image_url, i, param_str)
    else:
        line = "      {{ name: '{}', image_url: '{}', sort_order: {} }},".format(name, image_url, i)
    lines.append(line)
lines.append("    ],")
print('\n'.join(lines))

# 下载函数
def download(url, local_path):
    try:
        req = urllib.request.Request(url, headers={'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0'})
        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, context=ctx, timeout=30) as resp:
            with open(local_path, 'wb') as f:
                f.write(resp.read())
        size = os.path.getsize(local_path)
        return True, size
    except Exception as e:
        return False, str(e)

# 下载所有图片
dir = 'public/images/products/linear_guide'
for pid, info in images.items():
    for img in info['main'] + info['param']:
        url = f'{base}/upload/images/2020/12/25/{img}' if '12/25' in img or '12/28' in img and '2020' in img else f'{base}/upload/images/2020/12/17/{img}'
        # 判断路径
        if img.startswith('14') and len(img.split('_')) == 3:
            url = f'{base}/upload/images/2020/12/17/{img}'
        elif img.startswith('163') or img.startswith('14') and len(img.split('_')) == 3:
            # 需要判断月份
            if img in ['163620_41_296.jpg', '163555_41_294.jpg', '163530_41_292.jpg', '163454_41_290.jpg', 
                       '163436_41_288.jpg', '163420_41_286.jpg', '163402_41_284.jpg', '163337_41_282.jpg']:
                url = f'{base}/upload/images/2020/12/28/{img}'
            else:
                url = f'{base}/upload/images/2020/12/25/{img}'
        else:
            url = f'{base}/upload/images/2020/12/17/{img}'
        
        local = f'{dir}/{pid}_{img}'
        ok, result = download(url, local)
        if ok:
            print(f'OK {pid} {img} ({result} bytes)')
        else:
            print(f'ERR {pid} {img}: {result}')

print('\nDone!')

import os, re
from html.parser import HTMLParser

base = 'http://www.zuquchina.com'
products_info = [
    ('74', 'HGH-CA/HGH-HA 系列'),
    ('75', 'HGW-CA/HGW-HA 系列'),
    ('76', 'HGW-CB/HGW-HB 系列'),
    ('77', 'HGW-CC/HGW-HC 系列'),
    ('78', 'HGR-T 下锁式导轨'),
    ('79', 'EGH-SA/EGH-CA 系列'),
    ('80', 'EGW-SA/EGW-CA 系列'),
    ('81', 'EGW-SB/EGW-CB 系列'),
    ('82', 'RGH-CA/RGH-HA 系列'),
    ('83', 'RGL-CA/RGL-HA 系列'),
    ('84', 'RGW-CC/RGW-HC 系列'),
    ('85', 'RGR-T 下锁式滑轨'),
]

class ImgExtractor(HTMLParser):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.imgs = []
    def handle_starttag(self, tag, attrs):
        if tag == 'img':
            d = dict(attrs)
            src = d.get('src', '')
            if src.startswith('/upload/') and '085250_2_157.png' not in src and '21583110644.png' not in src:
                self.imgs.append(src)

for pid, name in products_info:
    path = f'/tmp/zq_details/{pid}.html'
    with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        html = f.read()
    
    # 提取 product-image-item 中的图片
    m1 = re.findall(r'<div class="product-image-item">\s*<img src="([^"]+)"', html)
    # 提取 product-content 中的图片
    m2 = re.findall(r'<div class="product-content">(.*?)</div>\s*</div>\s*<div class="row pageturning"', html, re.S)
    content_imgs = []
    if m2:
        ext = ImgExtractor()
        ext.feed(m2[0])
        content_imgs = ext.imgs
    
    print(f"{pid} {name}")
    print(f"  主图: {m1}")
    print(f"  参数图: {content_imgs}")
    print()
PYEOF

    try:
        req = urllib.request.Request(url, headers={'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0'})
        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, context=ctx, timeout=30) as resp:
            with open(local_path, 'wb') as f:
                f.write(resp.read())
        size = os.path.getsize(local_path)
        print(f'OK {pid} {fname} ({size} bytes)')
    except Exception as e:
        print(f'ERR {pid} {fname}: {e}')

with open('src/data/products.ts', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:

new_url = 'https://miaoda-conversation-file.cdn.bcebos.com/user-bpz5lndnjoxs/app-cku4hf2twpvl/20260703/IMG_0310副本_1783065386381.jpg'

# 替换 id: 1 分类下所有 sub_products 的 image_url
import re
pattern = r"(id: 1,.*?)sub_products: \[.*?RGR-T 下锁式滑轨', image_url: '[^']+', sort_order: 12, param_images: \[[^\]]+\] \},\n    \],"

def repl(m):
    block = m.group(0)
    # 替换所有 image_url
    block = re.sub(r"image_url: '[^']+'", f"image_url: '{new_url}'", block)
    return block

new_content = re.sub(pattern, repl, content, count=1, flags=re.S)

with open('src/data/products.ts', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    f.write(new_content)

print('Updated sub_products image_url to user image')
PYEOF
